class=\"modal-header\">\n                        <h4 class=\"modal-title\">How ShareTrips works?</h4>\n                    </div>\n                    <div class=\"modal-body\">\n                        <iframe height=\"100\" width=\"100\" rrc=\"//www.youtube.com/embed/vMdWx9adFDA\" seamless=\"\" allowfullscreen=\"\" style=\"border:0;\"></iframe>\n                    </div>\n                </div><!-- /.modal-content -->\n            </div><!-- /.modal-dialog -->\n        </div><!-- /.modal -->\n\n\n        <div class=\"modal fade\" id=\"help-modal\">\n            <div class=\"modal-dialog\">\n                <div class=\"modal-content\">\n                    <div class=\"modal-header\">\n                        <button type=\"button\" class=\"btn close\" data-dismiss=\"modal\"><span class=\"icon\" aria-hidden=\"true\"></span><span class=\"sr-only\">Close</span></button>\n                    </div>\n                    <div class=\"modal-body\">\n                        <h4 class=\"modal-title\">Help</h4>\n                        <ol id=\"help\">\n                            <li class=\"panel\">\n                                <a data-toggle=\"collapse\" data-parent=\"#help\" href=\"#help-1\">How does ShareTrips work?</a>\n                                <div id=\"help-1\" class=\"collapse\">\n                                    ShareTrips works like other online travel websites, but with unique features to make it easier for you to plan and book a trip with multiple travel companions. With ShareTrips, you can:\n                                    <ul>\n                                        <li>Screen share your webpage in real time with your travel companions. Your travel companions will view the same webpage you’re viewing.</li>\n                                        <li>Interact with the same webpage as your travel companions. Anyone viewing your webpage can start a new search, select a search result and navigate through the ShareTrips website without having to transfer control of the webpage.</li>\n                                        <li>Instant Message (IM) and Video Conference with your travel companions right from the ShareTrips webpage.</li>\n                                    </ul>\n                                </div>\n                            </li>\n                            <li class=\"panel\">\n                                <a data-toggle=\"collapse\" data-parent=\"#help\" href=\"#help-2\">How does screen sharing work?</a>\n                                <div id=\"help-2\" class=\"collapse\">\n                                    You can share your ShareTrips webpage in two ways.\n                                    <ul>\n                                        <li>Click the Facebook button on the left hand side of the webpage to bring up a list of your Facebook friends and message them directly through Facebook. </li>\n                                        <li>You will be asked to logon to Facebook if you are not already logged in. Your friends will receive a message on Facebook with a link to view your webpage. Once clicked, your friends will be viewing your webpage.</li>\n                                        <li>Click the orange button with the 8 digit ShareCode to bring up a dialog box. Copy and paste the URL containing your ShareCode and email or instant message the URL to your travel companions.</li>\n                                    </ul>\n                                </div>\n                            </li>\n                            <li class=\"panel\">\n                                <a data-toggle=\"collapse\" data-parent=\"#help\" href=\"#help-3\">What will my travel companions be able to see and do when I share my webpage?</a>\n                                <div id=\"help-3\" class=\"collapse\">\n                                    Your travel companions will only see your ShareTrips webpage and nothing else on your screen.\n                                    They will not see any other open browser tabs or other open windows on your computer screen.\n                                    Anyone sharing your webpage will be able to change the search destination, change search dates, and number of rooms and guests on your computer screen.\n                                    Anyone sharing your webpage will be able to interact with the search results on screen (e.g.; select a search result, view photos, view maps, select a room type, etc.)\n                                    Not all ShareTrips webpages are shared. For example, portions of the pages where you enter payment details are not shared with your travel companions. You can pay with confidence that your travel companions will not be able to see your credit card details.\n                                </div>\n                            </li>\n                            <li class=\"panel\">\n                                <a data-toggle=\"collapse\" data-parent=\"#help\" href=\"#help-4\">How do I communicate with my travel companions while sharing my webpage?</a>\n                                <div id=\"help-4\" class=\"collapse\">\n                                    You can communicate with your travel companions in two ways.\n                                    <ul>\n                                        <li>Instant Message/Chat. Use the integrated chat module on the right side of the ShareTrips website. Once sharing your webpage, just type a message to your travel companions into the chat window. Your message will appear instantly to everyone viewing your webpage.</li>\n                                        <li>Video Conferencing. Start a video conference right from the ShareTrips website. To start a video conference, click the Video button.\n                                            <ul>\n                                                <li>At the top of the browser window, your browser may require you to allow ShareTrips to access your video camera and microphone.</li>\n                                                <li>Once allowed, your image will appear in a thumbnail on the ShareTrips website. A thumbnail with your travel companion’s image will appear once they click the Video button on their computer.</li>\n                                                <li>To stop the video, click the Video button again.</li>\n                                                <li>To mute and unmute your microphone, click the Microphone button.</li>\n                                            </ul>\n                                        </li>\n                                    </ul>\n                                </div>\n                            </li>\n                            <li class=\"panel\">\n                                <a data-toggle=\"collapse\" data-parent=\"#help\" href=\"#help-5\">How can I make it easier for my travel companions to see what I am looking at on ShareTrips?</a>\n                                <div id=\"help-5\" class=\"collapse\">\n                                    When you share your webpage, you will see multiple cursors on your computer screen, one cursor for each of your travel companions.\n                                    By default, your cursor is labeled as “Friend”. Each viewer can label their cursor with their name by simply typing their name into the Name field in the Chat module.\n                                </div>\n                            </li>\n                            <li class=\"panel\">\n                                <a data-toggle=\"collapse\" data-parent=\"#help\" href=\"#help-6\">Why is the video conferencing not working?</a>\n                                <div id=\"help-6\" class=\"collapse\">\n                                    The video conferencing technology on ShareTrips is the latest in real time, in-browser communication technology and is not supported on older browsers and some operating systems. Instant Messaging/Chat is supported on systems that do not support video conferencing.\n                                    Video/Audio conferencing on ShareTrips works with the following systems:\n                                    <ul>\n                                        <li>Chrome</li>\n                                        <li>Firefox</li>\n                                        <li>Opera</li>\n                                        <li>Chromebooks</li>\n                                        <li>Android tablets/phones</li>\n                                    </ul>\n                                    Video/Audio conferencing is NOT supported on the following products:\n                                    <ul>\n                                        <li>Safari</li>\n                                        <li>iPads/iPhones</li>\n                                        <li>Internet Explorer</li>\n                                    </ul>\n                                </div>\n                            </li>\n                            <li class=\"panel\">\n                                <a data-toggle=\"collapse\" data-parent=\"#help\" href=\"#help-7\">How can I improve the audio quality when sharing my webpage?</a>\n                                <div id=\"help-7\" class=\"collapse\">\n                                    Audio quality will depend on many factors including the quality of your computer’s microphone and speakers, the quality of your travel companion’s computer microphone and speakers, and your internet connection. To improve the audio quality of your connections:\n                                    <ul>\n                                        <li>Use a headset.</li>\n                                        <li>If not using a headset, speak directly into your computer’s microphone.</li>\n                                        <li>Turn the volume up on your computer.</li>\n                                        <li>Mute your microphone and ask your travel companions to mute their microphones when not speaking.</li>\n                                    </ul>\n                                </div>\n                            </li>\n                            <li class=\"panel\">\n                                <a data-toggle=\"collapse\" data-parent=\"#help\" href=\"#help-8\">Can I use ShareTrips from a tablet or mobile phone? Do you have an App?</a>\n                                <div id=\"help-8\" class=\"collapse\">\n                                    Yes, you can use ShareTrips from a tablet or mobile phone. ShareTrips should work properly on any internet enabled device. Please note, that Video/Audio conferencing is not available on iOS devices at this time. ShareTrips does not currently have an app.\n                                </div>\n                            </li>\n                            <li class=\"panel\">\n                                <a data-toggle=\"collapse\" data-parent=\"#help\" href=\"#help-9\">Can I spread my payment across multiple people or credit cards?</a>\n                                <div id=\"help-9\" class=\"collapse\">\n                                    No. Although we currently allow you to share webpages with travel companions, you must select one person in your party to pay for the entire reservation. Payment needs to be made on one credit card.\n                                </div>\n                            </li>\n                            <li class=\"panel\">\n                                <a data-toggle=\"collapse\" data-parent=\"#help\" href=\"#help-10\">How do I get assistance with my booking?</a>\n                                <div id=\"help-10\" class=\"collapse\">\n                                    To get assistance with a booking, please call in the US and Canada: 1-800-916-4338 or in Europe: 00-800-11-20-11-40. Reference Promo Code 438685.\n                                </div>\n                            </li>\n                            <li class=\"panel\">\n                                <a data-toggle=\"collapse\" data-parent=\"#help\" href=\"#help-11\">How do I get assistance with my accessibility needs?</a>\n                                <div id=\"help-11\" class=\"collapse\">\n                                    Prior to completing your booking, you’ll be able to enter any special requests including accessibility needs. Look for the field labeled Special Requests.\n                                </div>\n                            </li>\n                            <li class=\"panel\">\n                                <a data-toggle=\"collapse\" data-parent=\"#help\" href=\"#help-12\">How do I cancel a booking?</a>\n                                <div id=\"help-12\" class=\"collapse\">\n                                    If you are still within the cancellation window for your booking, please call in the US and Canada: 1-800-916-4338 or in Europe: 00-800-11-20-11-40. Picking the right hotel for a group of people or your family can be nerve-wracking. From picking a hotel in the right location, to one with the right amenities and then making sure it fits into everyone’s budget, booking the right hotel on your own can be very stressful.</p>\n\n                        <p>Traditional online travel websites only allow one person to view a webpage and select a hotel, even if multiple people are traveling. With ShareTrips, our online collaboration tools allow all travelers in your party to interact with a shared web page and provide input to simplify the booking process for everyone traveling.</p>\n\n                        <p><img class=\"left\" src=\"img/ST-tagline4.png\" width=\"271\" height=\"21\" alt=\"Have a Say in Your Stay\">&nbsp;</p>\n\n                        <p style=\"color:grey;\">ShareTrips is a division of <i>RIV Tech, Inc.</i></p>\n\n                        <h4 class=\"modal-title\">Contact Us</h4>\n                        <p>ShareTrips is based in North Carolina. We have great people working for us around the world.</p>\n                        <table class=\"bcc\">\n                            <tbody><tr>\n                                    <td><span class=\"shareTripsOrange bold\">Our address:</span>\n                                        <br>6923 Shannon Willow Rd\n                                        <br>Charlotte, NC  28226-1331\n                                        <br><img id=\"map\" alt=\"Map\" src=\"img/map_sharetrips.gif\" width=\"430\" height=\"392\">\n<script>\nif (ST.machine.sdf) {\n    document.getElementById('map').src = 'img/map_staydrivefly.gif';\n} else {\n    document.getElementById('map').src = 'img/map_sharetrips.gif';\n}\n</script>\n                                    </td>\n                                    <td style=\"text-align:right; vertical-align:top;\"><span class=\"shareTripsOrange bold\">Our customer service number:</span>\n                                        <br>(800) 916-4338\n                                        <br>\n                                        <br><span class=\"shareTripsOrange bold\">Our email address:</span>\n                                        <br><a href=\"mailto:support@sharetrips.com\">support@sharetrips.com</a>\n                                    </td>\n                                </tr>\n                        </tbody></table>\n\n                        <h4 class=\"modal-title\">The Team</h4>\n\n                        <h5 class=\"modal-title\">Joe Lima</h5>\n\n                        <p>Joe Lima is a co-founder and CEO of ShareTrips. He has worked in the travel industry for over 10 years starting with the launch team of Hotwire.com. Prior to Hotwire, Joe served in various management and consulting roles at Excite.com, Accenture and EDS (now part of Hewlett-Packard).</p>\n\n                        <p>At Hotwire, Joe led the launch activities for Hotwire’s Flights and Hotels product in late 2000 and spearheaded the development of Hotwire’s first data warehouse. Joe has held various positions on both the technical and business side of the travel industry, most recently serving as Hotwire’s Senior Manager for Core and Emerging Businesses. In that role, he was responsible for managing Hotwire’s product relationship with external partners such as United Airlines and Kayak as well as internal partners, Expedia and Hotels.com. He managed products generating over $800M in annual gross bookings and $30M in net revenue for Hotwire.</p>\n\n                        <p>Joe holds a Bachelor of Arts degree in Economics from the University of California, San Diego. Joe is passionate about travel, technology, animal welfare and education. Joe is the benefactor of the Joseph Lima Scholarship at UCSD providing financial assistance to students of limited means who are the first in their family to attend college.</p>\n\n                        <p><a href=\"http://www.linkedin.com/in/joelima\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"cool shareTripsBlueLight bold\">Connect with Joe: <img alt=\"LI\" src=\"img/li.png\" style=\"vertical-align:text-bottom;\" width=\"17\" height=\"17\"></a></p>\n\n                        <h5 class=\"modal-title\">Lee Heyne</h5>\n\n                        <p>Lee Heyne is a co-founder and CTO of ShareTrips. Lee is the developer and integrator of much of the online collaboration technology that powers ShareTrips. Prior to helping found ShareTrips, Lee held a variety of lead technical positions at various start-ups as well as intern positions at Qualcomm, Boeing and Honeywell.</p>\n\n                        <p>Lee holds a Bachelor of Science degree in Engineering from Harvey Mudd College. He has traveled the world extensively, especially Southeast Asia where he practiced yoga while enjoying the region's great vegetarian cuisine.</p>\n\n                        <p><a href=\"http://www.linkedin.com/pub/lee-heyne/7/a24/9b1\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"cool shareTripsBlueLight bold\">Connect with Lee: <img alt=\"LI\" src=\"img/li.png\" style=\"vertical-align:text-bottom;\" width=\"17\" height=\"17\"></a></p>\n\n                        <h5 class=\"modal-title\">Josh Skoko</h5>\n\n                        <p>Josh Skoko is the Chief Marketing Officer for ShareTrips. He has worked in the travel industry for over 9 years with 15 years of experience in the online marketing channel.  At Hotwire, he was the Director of Online Marketing and Search Engine Marketing for seven years and significantly grew all aspects of the Hotwire Group’s online partnership marketing, affiliate marketing and search engine marketing programs. Josh also led all digital creative agency partnerships.</p>\n\n                        <p>Prior to Hotwire, Josh ran online marketing programs at Blue Nile and worked in media at Avenue A/Razorfish where he focused on brands like Expedia, Classic Vacations, David’s Bridal, Intuit, Eddie Bauer, and Spiegel.</p>\n\n                        <p>Josh received a BA in Business Administration with a concentration in Marketing from Western Washington University.</p>\n\n                        <p><a href=\"http://www.linkedin.com/pub/josh-skoko/8/8b8/a8\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"cool shareTripsBlueLight bold\">Connect with Josh: <img alt=\"LI\" src=\"img/li.png\" style=\"vertical-align:text-bottom;\" width=\"17\" height=\"17\"></a></p>\n\n                        <h5 class=\"modal-title\">Clem Bason</h5>\n\n                        <p>Clem Bason is an advisor to ShareTrips. He spent seven years at The Hotwire Group, four of them as President overseeing all aspects of the Hotwire.com, Travel Ticker, and CarRentals.com businesses.  Hotwire is the leading global online discount travel retailer, with over $2B in annual gross bookings, and operations in North America, Latin America, Europe, and Asia.  Prior to Hotwire, Clem was at Gap Inc., McKinsey &amp; Co., and Accenture.</p>\n\n                        <p>Clem holds a MBA from the University of California at Berkeley and a BA from the University of Delaware.  Clem is passionate about making travel easier and a better value for consumers and continues to invest his time helping companies that do so.</p>\n\n                        <p><a href=\"http://www.linkedin.com/pub/clem-bason/0/40b/b79\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"cool shareTripsBlueLight bold\">Connect with Clem: <img alt=\"LI\" src=\"img/li.png\" style=\"vertical-align:text-bottom;\" width=\"17\" height=\"17\"></a></p>\n\n                        <h5 class=\"modal-title\">Seth Strumph</h5>\n\n                        <p>Seth Strumph is an advisor to ShareTrips. The ShareTrips.com website (the “Site”) allows users to view and book travel products listed on the Site. When a user enters search parameters into the Site, the ShareTrips service matches available travel products from third party suppliers with the user’s request parameters. User’s may then share the results of their search in real time with their travel companions using ShareTrips’ patent pending Remote Interactive Viewing (RIV) technology (the “Service”). The primary user or the user’s travel companion may then choose to book a selected travel product through one of our third party suppliers. The terms “we” or “us” refers to ShareTrips, a service of RIV Tech, Inc., a Delaware Corporation and/or our subsidiaries and corporate affiliates. The terms “you” “user” and “users” refers to visitors to the Site who are searching, browsing and/or booking a reservation through the Site or through customer service agents.\n\n                        <h5 class=\"modal-title\">\n                        Agreement\n                        </h5>\n\n                        This Terms of Use Agreement (the “Agreement”) describes the terms on which you, as a user of the Site may access and use the Site and the Service. If you do not agree with the terms of this Agreement, including our Privacy Policy (which is incorporated into this Agreement) you should not use or access our Site or our Service. As a condition of using the Site, you warrant that you are at least 18 years of age and you possess the legal authority to create a legally binding obligation. We reserve the right to modify this Agreement at any time, and without prior notice, by posting amended terms on this Site. Your continued use of the Service indicates your acceptance of this Agreement and any amendments. The Site reserves the right to modify or discontinue, temporarily or permanently, the Site, any site features, benefits, rules or conditions, all without notice, even though such change may affect the way you use the Site. You agree that the Site will not be liable to you or any third-party for any modification or discontinuance of the Site or Service.\n\n                        <h5 class=\"modal-title\">\n                        Use Of Service\n                        </h5>\n\n                        As a user, you are responsible for maintaining the confidentiality of your searches when using the Service. You agree to only use the RIV technology with persons known to you and to not accept sharing requests from unknown persons. ShareTrips will not be liable for any loss or damage arising from your failure to comply with this notification requirement. These log files may automatically collect information such as how often a user visits the website, user IP address, and other browser-type related information, among other things. This information is used to better administer the Site as well as to enhance and improve the Service. A cookie is a piece of data stored on the user's computer tied to information about the user. We may use cookies to enable functionality such as for the Site to recall a user’s previous interaction with the Site. ShareTrips may use Web beacons (also known as clear gifs, pixel tags or action tags). Web beacons are tiny graphics with a unique identifier, similar to cookies, but are placed in the code of a page on the Site. We use Web beacons to monitor traffic patterns of users, to set or read cookies, to understand your interactions with our online advertisements displayed on a third-party website, and to monitor Site performance. We may also allow our service providers to use Web beacons.\n\n                        <h5 class=\"modal-title\">\n                        Click-Throughs\n                        </h5>\n\n                        We may track when a user clicks on links or buttons contained on the Site. We do not share personal information associated with these click-throughs.\n\n                        <h5 class=\"modal-title\">\n                        Using Your Information\n                        </h5>\n                        We use information from user interactions on the Site to monitor, maintain and improve the Service and the functioning of the Site. We also use information from user interactions to process your bookings through our third party suppliers. In the course of processing your bookings, we are required to share your information with our third party suppliers. Except as described below, ShareTrips does not rent, sell or disclose an individual user’s personal information to advertisers or other third parties. RIV Tech, Inc., the owner of ShareTrips.com, is the owner of any data about user behavior or characteristics that it derives from the Site. In the course of conducting normal business, ShareTrips will not disclose user personal information to any third party unless we believe that disclosure is necessary: (1) to conform to legal requirements or to respond to a subpoena, search warrant or other legal process received by ShareTrips; (2) to enforce the ShareTrips Terms of Use Agreement or to protect our rights; (3) to permit third party contractors, under obligations of confidentiality, to assist in the maintenance of the Site and the provision of the Services or (4) to protect the safety of the public and users of the Service. We further reserve the right to transfer user personal information in the event of a bankruptcy or a merger, acquisition, joint venture or other business combination involving us.\n\n                        <h5 class=\"modal-title\">\n                        Protecting Your Information\n                        </h5>\n                        ShareTrips takes precautions to insure that any user information is kept confidential. We use industry standard measures to protect user information that is stored within our database. We limit the access to your information to those employees who need access to perform their job function such as our customer service personnel. Please note that we cannot guarantee the security of user information. Unauthorized entry or use, hardware or software failure and other factors may compromise the security of user information at any time.\n\n                        <h5 class=\"modal-title\">\n                        Email Communication\n                        </h5>\n                        In the course of providing the Service, we may communicate with users via email.
